  </style><div class="tooltip-information-choice-enhance-apply fl">* Limited enrollment is an option for providers who will ONLY submit claims to and receive payments from Florida Medicaid managed care health plans.                

** Fee-for-service is a method of payment where the provider is paid a fee for each procedure performed and billed within the Medicaid policy limitations.   

*** This option is known as FULL enrollment.  Fully enrolled providers can participate in BOTH the network of a Medicaid health plan(s) as well as bill for services and receive payment directly from Medicaid.                                                               

**** Referring, Ordering, Prescribing, or Attending (ROPA) providers will not receive reimbursement for services.  A ROPA provider orders or refers patients, prescribes prescription drugs, and/or services as the attending practitioner in institutional settings for Medicaid recipients.  These providers may be identified as the ROPA provider on any professional, pharmacy, institutional, or dental claims.</div></div><span data-tip="true" data-for="Please select the option from below
